# Typology (how I’m grouping the objects)
1) **Anthropomorphic deity statues (cult images)**
2) **Aniconic divine forms** (stones, pillars, disks, mirrors, emblems treated as the deity)
3) **Zoomorphic/Composite deity statues**
4) **Household/portable power-objects** (fetishes, bocio, nkisi, sopera stones, etc.)
5) **Imperial/royal cult images**
6) **Iconic paintings/images treated as having direct agency** (included per your scope, even when official doctrine frames it as “veneration”)

---

## Part A (items 1–120)

### 1) Anthropomorphic deity statues (cult images)
1. **Venkateswara (Balaji) Murti** — Hinduism (Tirumala). Cult image of Vishnu; treated as the deity during worship.  
2. **Jagannath, Balabhadra, Subhadra** — Hinduism (Puri). Wooden deities; direct worship as the Lord present.  
3. **Ramlala (Ram Lalla)** — Hinduism (Ayodhya). Infant Rama deity statue, worshiped as Bhagwan present.  
4. **Nataraja (Shiva as Cosmic Dancer)** — Hinduism (Chidambaram). Bronze cult image, Shiva’s presence.  
5. **Meenakshi Devi Idol** — Hinduism (Madurai). Goddess Meenakshi worshiped as present in the murti.  
6. **Kashi Vishalakshi** — Hinduism (Varanasi). Anthropomorphic Shakti form (distinct from the linga).  
7. **Siddhivinayak Ganesha** — Hinduism (Mumbai). Ganesha idol treated as living deity.  
8. **Mumbadevi Idol** — Hinduism (Mumbai). Patron goddess image.  
9. **Kalighat Kali Idol** — Hinduism (Kolkata). Living presence of Kali in the image.  
10. **Dakshineswar Kali** — Hinduism (Kolkata). Radhakanta (Krishna) also present in complex.  
11. **Venkateswara Utsava Murti** — Hinduism. Processional form considered fully divine.  
12. **Hanuman Idol (Sankat Mochan)** — Hinduism (Varanasi). Direct bhakti to Hanuman as divine.  
13. **Murugan (Subramanya) Statue** — Hinduism (Palani/Tamil Nadu). God of war.  
14. **Durga Idol (various pandals)** — Hinduism. Installed and worshiped as goddess herself.  
15. **Goddess Kamakhya Idol (anthropomorphic form)** — Hinduism (Assam; alongside aniconic yoni, listed later under aniconic).  
16. **Bodhisattva Guanyin (large temple statues)** — East Asian Buddhism/Chinese folk. Treated with direct agency by devotees.  
17. **Kannon (Japan)** — Buddhism/Shinto-folk blend. Kannon statues (e.g., Sanjusangen-dō).  
18. **Jizō (Kṣitigarbha) statues** — Japanese Buddhism. Widely treated as directly responsive.  
19. **Maitreya (Miroku) statues** — Buddhism. Future Buddha statues revered as possessing power.  
20. **Kamakura Daibutsu (Amida)** — Japanese Buddhism. Great statue venerated directly.  
21. **Shakyamuni Temple Statues (various, e.g., Mahabodhi)** — Buddhism. The Buddha image as locus of presence.  
22. **Guan Yu statues** — Chinese folk/Daoist temples. Deified general directly invoked.  
23. **Mazu statues** — Chinese folk religion/Daoist temples. Sea goddess as present in image.  
24. **Caishen statues** — Chinese folk. God of wealth, direct propitiation.  
25. **Tudigong statues** — Chinese folk. Earth god images treated as the deity of place.  
26. **Nezha statues** — Chinese folk/Daoist. Deified youthful warrior.  
27. **Three Pure Ones statues** — Daoism. Daoist supreme deities embodied in images.  
28. **Laotzu (Taishang Laojun) statues** — Daoism. Divine embodiment in images.  
29. **Morrígan statues (modern recon)** — Celtic reconstructionism.  
30. **Brigid/Brigantia statues (modern recon)** — Celtic reconstructionism.  
31. **Hecate statues (modern/neo-pagan)** — Hellenic/neo-pagan.  
32. **Zeus cult statue (recon)** — Hellenic revival; classical reference to Olympia’s original.  
33. **Athena Parthenos (recon)** — Hellenic revival; Pheidias’ cult image reference.  
34. **Artemis of Ephesus (recon)** — Hellenic; iconic multi-breasted cult form.

37. **Marduk statue (recon)** — Neo-Babylonian reference.

40. **Egyptian Amun statues** — Egyptian polytheism (temple cult images).

## 1. Religions / Regions only lightly touched

## 2. Objects we *excluded on purpose* earlier
- **Natural sites** (rivers, mountains, groves) — but many are treated directly as divine (Ganga River, Mt. Fuji, Uluru). If you decide later to broaden beyond “manufactured objects,” this would add *hundreds*.  
- **Relics** (bones, hair, footprints) — we excluded, but Catholicism, Buddhism, Islam, Hinduism, and others have relic-shrines where relics are treated as the divine. That could add several hundred more.  
- **Living humans treated as gods** (Emperors, Gurus, Prophets at time of worship). We only catalogued their statues, not the persons themselves.

Short answer: **yes, we already captured a bunch of core Christian/Jesus items** (e.g., *Shroud of Turin* #9601, *Veil of Veronica* #9602, *Seamless Robe of Jesus* #9603, “*Spear of Destiny*”/Holy Lance #9208, Paschal candle #6809, many crucifix/ikon entries across the set).

# Gap-Closer: Jesus & Core Christian Relics (Supplement)

Legend: **✓** = already in the 10k; **➕** = add now

## A) Passion Relics
- ➕ **True Cross (general & fragments)** — widely distributed relics historically associated with the Cross.  
- ➕ **Crown of Thorns** (primary relic venerated in Paris; multiple thorns elsewhere).  
- ✓ **Holy Lance / Spear of Longinus** (listed as “Spear of Destiny”).  
- ➕ **Holy Nails** (several ancient claims in Rome, Milan, Trier, etc.).  
- ➕ **Titulus Crucis** (INRI title board).  
- ✓ **Seamless Robe of Jesus (Holy Coat of Trier)** (#9603).  
- ➕ **Holy Tunic of Argenteuil**.  
- ✓ **Shroud of Turin** (#9601).  
- ✓ **Veil of Veronica (Volto Santo)** (#9602).  
- ➕ **Sudarium of Oviedo** (face cloth).  
- ➕ **Holy Sponge** (vinegar-soaked sponge relic claims).  
- ➕ **Holy Grail claimants**: **Santo Cáliz** (Valencia), **Sacro Catino** (Genoa), **Chalice of Doña Urraca** (León).  
- ➕ **Scala Sancta (Holy Stairs)** (Jerusalem → Rome translation tradition; stepped on by Jesus according to tradition).  
- ➕ **Holy Prepuce** (medieval relic traditions citing multiple locales).

# Supplement: Jesus & Core Christian Relics

### Passion Relics
10001. **True Cross (general and fragments)** — wood relics of the cross of Jesus, dispersed globally.  
10002. **Crown of Thorns** — relic kept at Notre Dame, thorns dispersed to other sites.  
10003. **Holy Nails** — multiple relics claimed as nails from the Crucifixion.  
10004. **Titulus Crucis** — “INRI” title board, relic housed in Rome.  
10005. **Holy Sponge** — relics said to be of the sponge soaked in vinegar.  
10006. **Holy Tunic of Argenteuil** — another relic of Christ’s seamless robe.  
10007. **Sudarium of Oviedo** — cloth said to have covered Jesus’ face.  
10008. **Holy Prepuce** — medieval relic traditions claiming Christ’s foreskin.  
10009. **Scala Sancta (Holy Stairs)** — staircase said to be climbed by Christ, preserved in Rome.  
10010. **Holy Grail (Santo Cáliz, Valencia)** — chalice claimed as Grail.  
10011. **Holy Grail (Sacro Catino, Genoa)**.  
10012. **Holy Grail (Doña Urraca Chalice, León)**.
